bernards_star_system = {
	name = "NAME_Barnard's_Star"
	class = sc_m
	usage_odds = 9999
	spawn_chance = 9999
	max_instances = 1
	flags = { sol_sector }
	init_effect = {
		every_neighbor_system = {
			set_star_flag = empire_cluster



		}

		create_dust_clouds = yes
	}

	planet = {
		count = 1
		class = star
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = 30
		has_ring = no
	}

	change_orbit = { min = 20 max = 60 }

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		flags = { hot_zone }

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 15 max = 20 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = 1
		orbit_distance = { min = 25 max = 30 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}

	planet = {
		count = 1
		orbit_distance = { min = 30 max = 35 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 35 max = 40 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 40 max = 50 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 50 max = 60 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}

	neighbor_system = {
		distance = { min = 10 max = 50 }
		initializer = "altair_system"
	}
	neighbor_system = {
		distance = { min = 10 max = 50 }
		initializer = "xi_bootis_system"
	}
}

alpha_centauri_system = {
	name = "NAME_Alpha_Centauri"
	class = sc_trinary_1
	usage_odds = 9999
	spawn_chance = 9999
	max_instances = 1
	flags = { sol_sector }
	init_effect = {
		every_neighbor_system = {
			set_star_flag = empire_cluster



		}

		create_dust_clouds = yes
	}
	flags = { binary_system }

	planet = {
		name = "NAME_Rigil_Kentaurus"
		count = 1
		class = pc_g_star
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1

		has_ring = no
	}

	change_orbit = 20

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 15 max = 20 }

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = 1
		orbit_distance = { min = 20 max = 25 }
		class = "pc_gas_giant"
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		entity = "gas_giant_16_entity"
		size = 36

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = 1
			orbit_distance = 6
			class = ideal_design_class
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			size = { min = 12 max = 18 }

			init_effect = {
				set_planet_flag = prescripted_ideal
			}
		}

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_distance = 6
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			size = 14
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = 1
		orbit_distance = { min = 25 max = 30 }

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = 1
		orbit_distance = { min = 30 max = 35 }

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 35 max = 40 }

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 40 max = 50 }

		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		name = "NAME_Alpha_Centauri_B"
		count = 1
		class = pc_k_star
		orbit_distance = 160
		orbit_angle = 40
		size = 27
		has_ring = no

		planet = {
			name = "NAME_Alpha_Centauri_B_I"
			class = pc_molten
			size = 18
			orbit_distance = 65
			flags = { hot_zone }
		}
		planet = {
			name = "NAME_Alpha_Centauri_B_II"

		}

			name = "NAME_Alpha_Centauri_B_III"

			size = 35
			orbit_angle = 330
			orbit_distance = 30
		}
	}


	planet = {
		name = "NAME_Proxima_Centauri"
		count = 1
		class = pc_m_star
		orbit_distance = 35
		orbit_angle = 130
		size = 20
		has_ring = no

		planet = {
			name = "NAME_Proxima_Centauri_I"

		}

		planet = {
			name = "NAME_Proxima_Centauri_II"
			class = pc_gas_giant

			orbit_distance = 25
		}
